Key functions:\\n  - `Authenticate`: Extracts the token from the `Authorization` header (Bearer or Basic auth with `api_key` username), calls `getAPIKey` to resolve and validate it, then calls `validateApiKey`.\\n  - `getAPIKey` / `getFromToken` / `getFromTokenLegacy`: Dispatches token lookup based on the `gl` prefix (new format uses `satokengen`, legacy uses `apikeygen`).\\n  - `validateApiKey`: Enforces key expiration (`Expires` field), revocation (`IsRevoked`), org-ID mismatch, and ensures the key is linked to a service account (plain API keys without service accounts are rejected).\\n  - `Hook`: Asynchronously updates the `last_used_at` timestamp after successful auth.\\n  - `getTokenFromRequest`: Parses `Authorization` header for Bearer or Basic tokens.\\n- `pkg/services/authn/clients/api_key_test.go`: Unit tests for the above.\\n- `pkg/services/authn/authnimpl/registration.go`: Registers `ProvideAPIKey` as an authn client via `authnSvc.RegisterClient`.\\n\\n**API Key Service Interface and Model:**\\n- `pkg/services/apikey/apikey.go`: `Service` interface with methods `GetAllAPIKeys`, `AddAPIKey`, `GetApiKeyByName`, `GetAPIKeyByHash`, `UpdateAPIKeyLastUsedDate`.\\n- `pkg/services/apikey/model.go`: `APIKey` struct with fields for expiry (`Expires *int64`), revocation (`IsRevoked *bool`), and service account linkage (`ServiceAccountId *int64`). Used for new API keys.\\n- `pkg/components/apikeygen/apikeygen.go`: Legacy base64-JSON API key generation and validation (`IsValid` hashes and compares).\\n\\n**Scope Enforcement:**\\n- `pkg/services/serviceaccounts/api/api.go`: The service account REST API enforces RBAC scope checks on all token management endpoints (e.g., `EvalPermission(serviceaccounts.ActionRead, serviceaccounts.ScopeID)` for listing tokens, `ActionWrite` for creating/deleting tokens) using `accesscontrol.Middleware`.\\n- `pkg/services/serviceaccounts/api/token.go`: Token creation (`CreateToken`) enforces max `SecondsToLive` from config and a day-based expiry limit (`SATokenExpirationDayLimit`). `hasExpired` checks expiry for token listing display.\\n- `pkg/services/accesscontrol/filter.go`: Generic RBAC scope filter (`Filter`, `ParseScopes`) used throughout the access control system to restrict resource visibility based on scope wildcards or specific IDs.\\n- `pkg/services/accesscontrol/migrator/migrator.go`: `MigrateRemoveDeprecatedPermissions` removes legacy `apikeys:*` permissions from the database.\\n\\n**DTO:**\\n- `pkg/api/dtos/apikey.go`: `NewApiKeyResult` DTO returned when a token is created.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":3,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1227,"cache_read_input_tokens":57735,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":1227,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"d8d231a9-45d4-43f3-9712-b0e15ba6c32f","uuid":"2de0819d-4adc-4a1a-804c-e2ff72fdca73"}

\"pkg/services/serviceaccounts/api/api.go\", \"symbol\": \"RegisterAPIEndpoints\"}\n  ],\n  \"text\": \"The API key authentication system in grafana/grafana is implemented across several layers:\\n\\n**Authentication Middleware (Entry Point):**\\n- `pkg/services/contexthandler/contexthandler.go`: The `ContextHandler.Middleware` is the HTTP middleware that initiates authentication for every request. It calls `authn.Authenticator.Authenticate`, which dispatches to the appropriate client.\\n\\n**API Key Authentication Client:**\\n- `pkg/services/authn/clients/api_key.go`: Core implementation. The `APIKey` struct implements `authn.HookClient` and `authn.ContextAwareClient`. Key functions:\\n  - `Authenticate`: Extracts the token from the `Authorization` header (Bearer or Basic auth with `api_key` username), calls `getAPIKey` to resolve and validate it, then calls `validateApiKey`.\\n  - `getAPIKey` / `getFromToken` / `getFromTokenLegacy`: Dispatches token lookup based on the `gl` prefix (new format uses `satokengen`, legacy uses `apikeygen`).\\n  - `validateApiKey`: Enforces key expiration (`Expires` field), revocation (`IsRevoked`), org-ID mismatch, and ensures the key is linked to a service account (plain API keys without service accounts are rejected).\\n  - `Hook`: Asynchronously updates the `last_used_at` timestamp after successful auth.\\n  - `getTokenFromRequest`: Parses `Authorization` header for Bearer or Basic tokens.\\n- `pkg/services/authn/clients/api_key_test.go`: Unit tests for the above.\\n- `pkg/services/authn/authnimpl/registration.go`: Registers `ProvideAPIKey` as an authn client via `authnSvc.RegisterClient`.\\n\\n**API Key Service Interface and Model:**\\n- `pkg/services/apikey/apikey.go`: `Service` interface with methods `GetAllAPIKeys`, `AddAPIKey`, `GetApiKeyByName`, `GetAPIKeyByHash`, `UpdateAPIKeyLastUsedDate`.\\n- `pkg/services/apikey/model.go`: `APIKey` struct with fields for expiry (`Expires *int64`), revocation (`IsRevoked *bool`), and service account linkage (`ServiceAccountId *int64`). Also defines error sentinels.\\n- `pkg/services/apikey/apikeyimpl/apikey.go`: `Service` implementation, delegates to `store` interface.\\n- `pkg/services/apikey/apikeyimpl/store.go`: Internal `store` interface definition.\\n- `pkg/services/apikey/apikeyimpl/xorm_store.go`: SQL-backed store. `AddAPIKey` computes the `Expires` timestamp from `SecondsToLive`. `UpdateAPIKeyLastUsedDate` updates the last-used timestamp.\\n- `pkg/services/apikey/apikeytest/fake.go`: Fake service for tests.\\n\\n**Token Generation (Key Format):**\\n- `pkg/components/satokengen/tokengen.go`: Generates and decodes modern `gl`-prefixed service account tokens (format `gl<serviceID>_<secret>_<checksum>`). Used for new API keys.\\n- `pkg/components/apikeygen/apikeygen.go`: Legacy base64-JSON API key generation and validation (`IsValid` hashes and compares).\\n\\n**Scope Enforcement:**\\n- `pkg/services/serviceaccounts/api/api.go`: The service account REST API enforces RBAC scope checks on all token management endpoints (e.g., `EvalPermission(serviceaccounts.ActionRead, serviceaccounts.ScopeID)` for listing tokens, `ActionWrite` for creating/deleting tokens) using `accesscontrol.Middleware`.\\n- `pkg/services/serviceaccounts/api/token.go`: Token creation (`CreateToken`) enforces max `SecondsToLive` from config and a day-based expiry limit (`SATokenExpirationDayLimit`). `hasExpired` checks expiry for token listing display.\\n- `pkg/services/accesscontrol/filter.go`: Generic RBAC scope filter (`Filter`, `ParseScopes`) used throughout the access control system to restrict resource visibility based on scope wildcards or specific IDs.\\n- `pkg/services/accesscontrol/migrator/migrator.go`: `MigrateRemoveDeprecatedPermissions` removes legacy `apikeys:*` permissions from the database.\\n\\n**DTO:**\\n- `pkg/api/dtos/apikey.go`: `NewApiKeyResult` DTO returned when a token is created.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
